            end

            end

            end   }
            0ACE: show_formatted_text_box "Public 1775 is not support this function, please wait for update!" 0x0ACE
        end 
        if  $TEMPVAR_X_COORD == 5

            else
                0ACE: show_formatted_text_box "You haven't enough money!" 0x0ACE
            end

:MISSION_STARTER
thread 'MISSION_STARTER'

:MISSION_STARTER_UPDATE
wait 0
IF
   not Actor.Dead($PLAYER_ACTOR)
jf @MISSION_STARTER_UPDATE
if not Player.WantedLevel(0) > 0
jf @MISSION_STARTER_UPDATE
if $ONMISSION == 0
jf @MISSION_STARTER_UPDATE
if
00FE:   actor $PLAYER_ACTOR sphere 1 in_sphere 1537.942 -1690.9958 13.5469 radius 1.0 1.0 1.0
then
    gosub @CreateMenuSelectYesOrNo
    0209: 10@ = random_int_in_ranges 3 6

    if MenuSelectedBool == true
    then
        start_mission 10@
    end
    wait 2000
end


goto @MISSION_STARTER_UPDATE

:Get_float_to_2number
0085: 11@ = 0@
008C: 10@ = float 11@ to_integer 
008D: 12@ = integer 10@ to_float 
0086: 13@ = 11@ // (float) 
0061: 13@ -= 12@ // (float) 
13@ *= 100.0 
008C: 14@ = float 13@ to_integer
if
    14@ < 0
then
14@ *= -1
end 
0AB2: ret 2 10@ 14@

:SHOW_GXT
thread 'SHOW_GXT' 
31@ = 0
jump @GXT_SCRIPT


:GXT_SCRIPT
05AA: 19@s = s$Add_Text // @s = 'short' 
33@ = 0 
10@ = 0 
11@ = 0 
0085: 18@ = 5@ // (int) 
27@ = 1
16@ = 0 
32@ = 0
01BD: 28@ = current_time_in_ms
01BD: 26@ = current_time_in_ms


:SHOW_GXT_56
wait 0
if 
    not $Clear_thread_texts == 1 
jf @Noname_3_12  
if or
801D:   not  33@ > 0@ // (int) 
0@ == -1 
jf @SHOW_GXT_137 
if 
not 10@ >= 254 
jf @SHOW_GXT_169 
10@ += 1
if 10@ >= 254
then
    10@ = 255
end 
jump @SHOW_GXT_169 

:SHOW_GXT_137
if 
10@ > 0 
jf @Noname_3_12 
10@ -= 1 
27@ = 0
jump @SHOW_GXT_169 

:SHOW_GXT_169
if 
1@ == 1 
jf @SHOW_GXT_215 
if 
    18@ > 0.0 
jf @Noname_3_12
01BD: 28@ = current_time_in_ms
0062: 28@ -= 26@  // (int)
0093: 28@ = integer 28@ to_float
28@ /= 100.0
28@ *= 2.0
0063: 18@ -= 28@  // (float)

01BD: 26@ = current_time_in_ms


:SHOW_GXT_215
03F0: enable_text_draw 1 
0349: set_text_draw_font 1 
033F: set_text_draw_letter_size 2@ 3@ 
if  31@ == 1
then
    0340: set_text_draw_RGBA 128 138 135 10@ 
else
    0340: set_text_draw_RGBA 255 255 255 10@ 
end

0342: set_text_draw_centered 1 
0343: set_text_draw_linewidth 600.0 
060D: draw_text_shadow 27@ rgba 0 0 0 255 
045B: draw_text_2numbers 4@ 18@ GXT 19@s number 6@ 7@
jump @SHOW_GXT_56 

:Noname_3_12  
end_thread

:PlayerAutoAddHealth
if and
    not 20@ >= 70
    20@ > 0
    not $GameMode == 2 
then
    if
      IsPlayerDownHealth == 0
    then
        if
           33@ > 2000
        then
            33@ = 0
            20@ = Actor.Health($PLAYER_ACTOR)
            20@ += 1
            Actor.Health($PLAYER_ACTOR) = 20@
        end
    else
        if
           33@ > 1000
        then
            33@ = 0
            20@ = Actor.Health($PLAYER_ACTOR)
            20@ -= 1
            Actor.Health($PLAYER_ACTOR) = 20@
        end
    end
end        
return




if 10@ >= 0
then
    045A: draw_text_1number 510.0 370.0 GXT 'H_MON1' number 10@
else
    045A: draw_text_1number 510.0 370.0 GXT 'H_MON2' number 10@
end 


:WhenPlayerHudMoneyAdded
033F: set_text_draw_letter_size 0.4 1.0
0340: set_text_draw_RGBA 255 255 255 255 
0342: set_text_draw_centered 1 
0343: set_text_draw_linewidth 600.0 
060D: draw_text_shadow 1 rgba 0 0 0 255
10@ = Player.Money($PLAYER_CHAR) 
                                             
if
  showPlayerMoneyAdd == 1
then
    hudmoneyshowtime -= 1
    if
       hudmoneyshowtime < 255
    then
        MoneyAddfade -= 5
        if MoneyAddfade <= 0
        then
            MoneyAddfade = 0
        end
    end
    if
      hudmoneyshowtime > 0
    then
        if 
          hudmoneyshowtime > 255
        then
            MoneyAddfade += 5
           if MoneyAddfade >= 255
           then
               MoneyAddfade = 255
           end
        end
        033F: set_text_draw_letter_size 0.4 2.0
        0340: set_text_draw_RGBA 255 255 255 MoneyAddfade 
        0342: set_text_draw_centered 1 
        0343: set_text_draw_linewidth 600.0 
        060D: draw_text_shadow 1 rgba 0 0 0 MoneyAddfade 
        081C: draw_text_outline 1 RGBA 0 0 0 MoneyAddfade 
        if 
           MoneyAddNumber > 0
        then
            045A: draw_text_1number 530.0 25.0 GXT 'H_M1' number MoneyAddNumber
        else             
            045A: draw_text_1number 530.0 25.0 GXT "H_M2" number MoneyAddNumber
        end
        if not $TPC_ADD_MONEY == 0
        then
            Player.Money($PLAYER_CHAR)  += $TPC_ADD_MONEY 
            
        end
        
        if MoneyAddNumber >= 100
        then                
            if  $TPC_ADD_MONEY == 0
            then  
                0085: 10@ = MoneyAddNumber 
                10@ *= -1
                Player.Money($PLAYER_CHAR)  += 10@ 
                05A9: s$SendInfoText = 'CHEATEK' // s$ 
                Actor.Health($PLAYER_ACTOR) = 0
                $TPC_ADD_MONEY = 0
            end
        end
    else
        showPlayerMoneyAdd = 0
        hudmoneyshowtime = 0
    end
end

10@ = Player.Money($PLAYER_CHAR) 
if
803B: not  10@ == PlayerHudMoney  // (int)
then
    MoneyAddfade = 75
    showPlayerMoneyAdd = 1
    hudmoneyshowtime = 400
    MoneyAddNumber = Player.Money($PLAYER_CHAR)
    0062: MoneyAddNumber -= PlayerHudMoney  // (int)
    PlayerHudMoney = Player.Money($PLAYER_CHAR)
end
return

                    0085: 924@ = 200@ 
                    0085: 946@ = 13@ 
                    923@ = 1
                else
                    04C4: store_coords_to 10@ 11@ 12@  from_actor $PLAYER_ACTOR with_offset 0.0 0.0 0.5 
                    04C4: store_coords_to $tempvar_Float_1 $tempvar_Float_2 $tempvar_Float_3 from_actor 200@ with_offset 0.0 0.0 0.0
                    050A: 922@ = distance_between_XYZ $tempvar_Float_1 $tempvar_Float_2 $tempvar_Float_3 and_XYZ 10@ 11@ 12@

                    0025:   921@ > 922@  // (float)
                    then
                        0086: 921@ = 922@ 
                        0085: 924@ = 200@   
                        0085: 946@ = 13@                  
                    end
                end
           end  
        end // for
        923@ = 0
        if not Actor.Dead(924@)   
        then  
            Actor.StorePos(924@, 10@, 11@, 12@)
            if
               Actor.Driving(924@)
            then
                
                986@ = Actor.CurrentCar(924@)

                  not Car.Wrecked(986@)

                    985@ = 1

                    0432: 953@ = get_actor_handle_from_car 986@ passenger_seat 1

                    003B:   924@ == 951@  // (int)

                        978@ = 10
                    end
                    if
                    003B:   924@ == 952@  // (int)
                    then
                        978@ = 0
                    end
                    if
                    003B:   924@ == 953@  // (int)
                    then
                        978@ = 1
                    end
                    if
                    003B:   924@ == 954@  // (int)
                    then
                        978@ = 2

                    985@ = 0
                end

                985@ = 0
